 With the implementation of this process, the problem of lack of money in the payment of wages in gram panchayats will also be eliminated
 is vyavastha se check jamaa karne evam check ke clearence sambandhi pareshaaniyon se mazdooree bhugtan main hone vaali anaavashyak deree ko roka ja sakegaa

 shuukravaar ko ghante se bhi zyaada chale vichaar-vimarsh ke baavjood dravid munetra kashgam (diemke) tathaa congress ke bich tamilnadu main aagaamee vidhansabha chunaav ke liye siton ko lekar samjhauta nahin ho paaya he

 vaise, congress ne philhal kaha he ki shuukravaar kii baithak sirf chunavi ranneeti par charchaa ke liye bulaai gai thi

" 
 
 " On the other hand, MK Stalin, son of m Karunanidhi, said, "both sides put their point
 
 
 ab congress apane netritv se vichaar-vimarsh kar dobaaraa baat karegi
 
 
 " haalanki emke stallin ne yah bataane se inkaar kar diya ki congress ko kitni siton kii peshkash kii gai thi, lekin diemke sutron kaa kahana he ki vah sankhya lagbhag 30 thi
 On the other hand, the demand of Congress for the election of 234 seats assembly was 63 seats, as they contested the same number of seats in the 2011 elections
 sutron ne bataaya ab congress un siton kii pahchaan karegi, jin par vah chunaav ladanaa chaahati he
 The dmk's main ally, the Congress, is demanding more seats because the DMK failed to include Captain Vijayakanth's DMDK in its alliance for the election
 dmdike buudhvaar ko hi diemke kii sari ummiido par tusharapaat karte hue peedbluef main shaamil ho gai, jo darasal chaar partiyon kaa gathbandhan he, jisaki vajah se rajya vidhansabha kaa chunaav chaturkniya ban gaya he
 But the Congress is also not in a position to exert much pressure because its performance in the 2011 elections was very disappointing

 varsh 2006 tak congress kii sthiti nateezon main tulanaatmak rup se behatar thi, kyonki unhen 48 siten di gai thim, or unhone 34 par jeet hasil kii thi

 -input bhashaa In the first half of the current financial year (2017-18), the country's public banks have announced a total loan waiver of Rs 55,356 crore to show their npas are strong
 sarkari bainkon dwaara corporate sector ko di gai yah karjamaafee pichley vitt varsh 2016-17 kii pehali chamahi ke dauraan 35,985 karod rupee kii karjamaafee kaa 54 fisadi he
 For the past ten years, government banks have been announcing loan waiver to improve their npas, despite this, there has been an increase in npas of banks continuously during ten years
 lihaaja, sawaal bainkon dwaara kiye ja rahe lone rhitoff par uth rahaa he
 Question 1: Will npas of banks continue to grow rather than ending this way of forgiving corporate debt? Question 2: Does the Central Reserve Bank and Central Government need to devise some other way to improve the financial condition of banks According to the information given to a newspaper under the Right to Information by the Reserve Bank of India, the public sector banks have made the problem of NPA to make their book keeping strong
 During the last ten years, in the name of fighting YA, the total debt of Rs
 3,60,912 crore has been worked out by resorting to loan write-off
 ise bhi padhein: karjamaafee ke khilaaf RBI-SBI? afasaron kii bayaanbaji ke mynearabiai dwaara di gai jaankaree ke mutabik das saal pehle vitt varsh 2007-08 main sarkari bainkon ne enpie khatm karne ke liye 8,09 karod rupee kii karjamaafee kii thi
 After this, more than this amount has been waived year after year
 vitt varsh 2009-10 ke dauraan 11,185 karod rupee to vitt varsh 2010-11 main 17,794 karod rupee kaa karj maaf kiya gaya he
 This annual loan waiver of corporate loans increased to Rs 27,231 crore in FY 2012-13
 vahiin 2014 main desh main nai sarkaar banane ke baad corporate karjamaafee kii is rakam main bada ijapha kiya gaya
 While the corporate debt of Rs 49,018 crore was waived in the financial year 2014-15, the total corporate debt of Rs 57,585 crore in the year 2015-16 was waived off (to be removed from the balance sheet of banks)
 vahiin beete varsh 2016-17 main yah record str 77,123 karod rupee kii karjamaafee ban gai
 At the same time, in the current financial year, this amount has crossed the figure of 55,356 crore
 kya he lone rhitoff?bainkon ke enpie main corporate sector ko diya gaya karj rahata he
 When the companies are unable to repay even the interest on the loan taken from the bank and the bank's principal money starts sinking, the bank termes the loan as NPA (non Performing Asset)
 vahiin enpie kii samasya ko nipataane ke liye karj lene vaali company ko diwalia ghoshit karne kii prakriya main daal diya jaataa he
 The process of auctioning the bank of the assets of the company prepared by the bank's loan goes ahead
 ise bhi padhein: raghuram rajan bole- sarkaar kaa naukar nahin hota rigerv bank kaa governralihaaja, lone rhitoff ke jariye sarkari bank apane balanceshit se un companiyon ke karj ko mitaa dete hai jisase unka bahikhaata durust ho jaae or nuksaan chhip jaae
 But this does not affect the process of recovery of loans by banks
 bahikhaata durust hone ke baad karj kii recovery se aane vaale paise ko aage chalakar bank kii kamai main jod diya jaataa he
 The biggest benefit to banks by fixing bookkeeping is in giving new loans as any bank can give loans up to the limit set by the Reserve Bank
 corporate karjamaafee par kya kahata he rigerv bank?rigerv bank kah chukaa he ki desh ke sarkari bank apni balanceshit ko acha dikhaane ke liye lagaataar lone rhitoff kaa sahaara liya he
 According to RBI, recourse to loan write-offs is taken at a time when the debt in banks' books starts increasing and due to poor balance sheets in giving new loans to it
 kyon nahin khatm lone rhitoff se enpie?vittiya jaankaron kaa maananaa he ki yah ek aam dharna he ki lone rhitoff paardarshita kii kami he or iske jariye sarkari khajaane kaa durupyog kiya jaataa he
 According to a statement by a former Reserve Bank official, banks should try to eliminate NPA by using the loan writeoff process once in 5 to 10 years
 lekin beete das saal ke dauraan kendra sarkaar ke faisle se sarkari bank prati varsh lone rhitoff kaa istemaal kar rahe hai
 According to the Reserve Bank, loan writeoff should be done for small amount of loan, but according to the data released for the last ten years, public sector banks have increased the amount of loan writeoff continuously
